in indoor and outdoor sporting activities*

characteristics**:

different from the material of the sole.

part;

Footnotes to ex HS code 6403 91, 6403 99:
* Footwear made of genuine leather for use in indoor
and outdoor sporting activities means tennis shoes,
basketball shoes, gym shoes, training shoes and like,
that have the upper of the shoe consisting of not less
than 50% of genuine leather, except footwear worn
mainly or exclusively for walking, trekking, hiking,
alpinism.
** Preferential tariff treatment shall be granted in case
of the fulfilment of all of the following conditions:
- the additional mark «Sporting footwear» in box 8 of
the Certificate of Origin, and
- the specific description demonstrating the type of
sporting activity and technical features of the footwear
indicated in an additional sheet to the Certificate of
Origin
